  * grade_story_102.txt (grade=4.3)
    The story relies heavily on telling rather than showing, particularly regarding the prophecy and Finch's mission. The central conflict remains abstract, and while there are attempts at symbolism with the key, these elements don't coalesce into a meaningful theme. The ending lacks impact, offering resolution through intention rather than action.

The conflict is entirely internal and lacks specificity, resulting in a story that feels more like a motivational sketch than a fully realized narrative.
